Machu Picchu ikubvwa ndi mitengo yachepa yomwe ili Intihuatana, Mbuyi ya Moto, ndi Chimbengo cha Zikama zitatu.
Zimene zambiri za mayiko a ku chilimwe cha chifukwa ichi zikubedwa potero kuti zipeze zinziko zambiri za ziti zinali zikukhalapo mwachipangwa.
Ku 1976, zambise cha miti cha Machu Picchu 30% chinkhalidwa, ndipo kuyerekesa kumadza pang'ono kachikhalidwe.
Mwuoyo, mfumu mwa zinthu zofotokozera mwa msinga oyambira m'dziko lapansi ndi 35mm, yomwe ili kukhalabe makhodi aukulu wa zinthu zofotokozera za zithunzi za zamanzere pamene zinthu izi zinali zoyenera kwambiri.
Kulipezekera kulimene kusikula tsiku lachikwenye, koma zomwe zimakopa kwambiri ndikutsumba kwake kumadvetsetsa monga zovomerezeka za zinthu zokonga zofotokozera monga zinthu zofotokozera za kamera zamadzidzi.
Mizini ya 35mm, mliyenga, kuona muliwenga, ili imene imina 36mm m'kulingo ndi 24mm m'kulingo kwina.
Kweru ka mtunduwo (kugathilitsa pa mayi cha mayi cha zimizi ziwiri kuti zipekhithe) kwachifukwa imathandizira kuti ikhale 3:2.
Zimene zambiri zamayiko (mungwe mwa zamayiko za APS, monga chitsanzo) zimakhala zosagwirika pa kapena zikukhalapo mwachinsoko pa zovomerezeka izzi.
Ngozo yomwe imadwalitsidwa kwambili ndipo imadwalitsidwa kuwonjezwa kwa zokometeka, kulengeza mfulirizi wambiri ndipo ikulenga kuwumira pazikhalikhali ponse pamene ikugwira chiyembekezo cha nkhani m'zambanizi.

Mizimu ya mphampho yake yokongola idachitika kuwoza anthu alonse, ku chikalangano chongwe ndi anthu osabwera.
Kodi m'mene anthu asankha kulimbana ndi Khristu, limodzi monga zifukwa zambiri, ndi kuti kudya kwachikhalidwe kunalondera zisoni ndi ubwino, ndipo ndalama zomwe zamagwiritsidwa ntchito ndi kulimba kwa Nyengwe ili zikhalapo monga chifukwa ichi.
Mfumu wa chikhisitu chomwe chinali m'Roma kwa zaka zambiri za zigawi zambiri za miselamulo, ndi kuwonekera kwa mphampho ndi ndau zambiri, kunadi kunathandiza owerenga okuchepetsa mliyengu ukugwirika m'chikhisitu ichi.
Zikhala kutenga kuluka kwa zokambira, Zabwina zikhulupiritsa chikalatano cha malo okhala ndi mafunde a Germany.
Mvekero wa chyankiko ichi wachula, kukankuka zinthu zoyengerera ndipo zinthu zolonjeza za milenti ndipo za mitengo, koma izi zinkukamba ndikukumva ndikukana malamowa okugwiritsa ntchito ndodi okukhulupirika kwambiri m'chilimwe cha zokometeka zowamba ziwiri.
Bhitaniya inaba chikalamo m'zambiseza kukambiza mafunde a zonse za madalima, zimavikira kulenga zambiseza ngakhale mafunde osati a chikalamo.
Chifukwa chifukwa kukula ukukwana pa njira iyi, Germany inlitenga kuti zimatha kusukirwa mwachitsata m'zwingano zake za mikudya ya mayi-mayi.
Mpamene m'ziko la 1920, zifingo zokwanjira za anthu ashake ndi ma chikale ndi kukuluwira.

Kupezeka kwa chiyembekezo, ntchito zinali zopulutsidwa kwa zimodera zonse zamphamvu zamanga, zomwe zinali zikulupirika kwambiri ndipo zinali zokwanira.
Kumene kuli nthawi yansya kwa achipungira, chifukwa anthu ankakhala ankagwiritsa ntchito zinthu zokwanira kapena zinthu zosayenera kupanga zogwiritsa ntchito zawo.
Kusindika kwa Zomwe Zinali Zokometeka za Chitchitchi kwa France kumathandizakezera mitengo yambiri ya anthu osayenera osayenera osakhulupirika mchivukichi mchithu chachitatu ku kuyamba zokometeka zawo.

Chifukwa omwingi aamikazi ndi anthu ofunika kwambiri, olemba blogu amapewa kusowa chifukwa chokwanjira, ndipo amapewa kukamba.
Kukhulusa mapo blogo "kumapangitsa achuluka zambiri za dziko lalikulu." Kuzama kofuna kuwonesa chifukwa chotseka cha anthu ofunsa kumapangitsa achuluka kukonza ndipo kukula.
Kukhulusa zifotokozo kuli chifukwa chokha ndikuwononga chitsanzo chomwe chimathandiza anthu kukuthengetsa zinthu zamfano, ndipo chimamugwiritsa ntchito ophungula kuti ziwalele zinthu zowona kuwononga m'fundo osayenera mwachindule pa msanga wochitala.
Kukhuzana kwa zikhalidwe zoyenera za zikhalidwe zofotokozera ("blogs") kungathandize ophungula kuphunzira kubwiga komanso kusanza; chifukwa ophungula amawonera monga ofuna kusonyeza monga ali m'ntchito ndi izo zozenga zinkachitika ndi anthu osowa, komanso kuchepetsa monga ali ndi zomwe amaganiza za zinthu zosonkana (Oravec, 2002).
Ottawa ndi capitale ya ku Canada yomwe ili yosangalala, ikuchuluka mfa a zamalendo ndi mmuzimu omwe amawononga mphamumu wa ku Canada pamene pa saku.
Kufuka kulanga ku Niagara Falls, ndipo kulanga kumphukusikira ndi kukhalapo kwa ubwino wambiri wa chibwino cha nthawi ya Muskoka ndi kuwonyeza kwake.
Zambiso zonse izzi ndi zimene zimalepheretsa kulimbitsa Ontario ngati zinthu zomwe zimagwiritsidwa ntchito kwambiri zokometsera Chivhangeri ku anthu osiyanasiyana.
Zikhala mifukwi yambiri ku kudenga kupwila, ndipo monga m'ntchito imene kusowa anthu, komanso kukula kwa mnkhondo wa dzira.
Kufanidwa kwa zovomerezeka za zomwe zili msanga kuwonetsa zinthu zochokera ku anthu ambiri: Amene ali ndi chuma cha African American m'US ali achikhalira pansi pa anthu achi Canadian.
Mafumu a Afrika posoni amali m'Oluhuru la Mlombela, pansi pa chifukwa cha Mulanje wa Afrika atchuluka.
Madzagari ndiyo yakazara kwambira, ndipo ndi chini chomwe chakukhalapo kwa nyumba zikabu.
Zimwe zikulu za maphiyo amachete amene ali ndi chuma, zimakhala zonenekera, kapita zikugwirana ntchito ndi France, ndipo zimapangidwira monga malo owiratira za zinthu zosidze.
Abale Abarabu ankhamphula Islam mwachikulu mwachikulu m'dziko, ndipo inkadwalidwa mwachikulu m'Comoros ndi Mayotte.
Kukhutsukuka kwa za chiyenerera cha Europa ndi kuchepetsa mphamumu kunayamba m'nthware ya chinkhama cha 15, ponena za chizindikiro cha wanyanjala wa ku Europa wakutsogonzera Vasco da Gama atuka njira ya Cape ku ku India.
Ku chikhulu, chikhongono ichitikira ku Sahel, ndipo ku josoni ndi kukhulapa ikitikira ku Nkhotero.
Magalati: Amene zithanditsidwa kuti zikhala zambiri zokwera ndikowala ziuoneka zikakhulupiriza kuti zili ndi mwane, ngakhale ngati zili zikumeneku.
Kuli chifukwa chakakhala chosadandaula kusowa kuluka mwezi (komabe ngati si mwezi omwe amveli zinthu zozengerera kwambiri).
Abwanuza amafiti ashalibeza kuti kafukuswe ka zamene kumakhulpika mbatava kaatandala ka zikwerero kaikhulupirika ndi chinyadiki, ndipo kukulu kwa kuchepetsa, kuchepetsa mphamvu, ndi zina zotero sikuli chizindikiro cha chiyembekezo.
Zikhale zikale, zikhale zikale kuchepetsa anzibiri, ndipo musitale zikhala zikuyimbira (zinkakhala zikukhalidwa kapena zikukhalidwa, zinapangidwa zikukhalidwa).
Mwezi wotendekera wa Casablanca uchedikidwa ndi amene ankakora zikanyala za Berber pa msinga wa chivula chachi 10 BCE, ndipo unagwiritsidwa ntchito ndi achi Phoenician, achi Roman, ndi achi Merenid ngati malo opekera opadera omwe ankadziwika ngati Anfa.

Sultani wa Morocco anapanga chisoko chomwe chinali chokaduka chokaduka, ndipo chinalidziwika ngati Daru l-Badya, koma Spanish okhudza anapereka dzina la Casablanca ponse anapanga malo okhudza makhalidwe aogulitsa apo.
Casablanca ndi m'malo osaphulikana kwambiri okupanga zofunikira m'chimodzimodzimodwa cha Morocco.
Muli ku ndalama za madini akale, kukudaula mibiya yopita pita ya Morocco muli chisoni, monga tagine, zambara, zinthu zam'mbiri, hookah, ndi mabiya osiyanasiyana, koma zonse izi ndi za ozongola.
Goma ndi chilandwe cha ozongola cha Zamboja ya Congo ya Mbuyi, m'chiyenda chokale cha Rwanda.
M'2002, Goma inalipezeka ndi माफwayi a chimbadwa ochokera ku chimbadwa cha Nyiragongo, zomwe zimaperekedwa m'makholo a malo a mitengo ya chiyenda achitunda, makamaka malo achikhalidwe.
Pamene Goma ndi yokonzeka, zovisitira kutskitsika kwa Goma zimafuna kufufuza kuti zikhale zizada ndi zikhalidwe za chisowelo chomwe chimachitika m'chikhalidwe cha North Kivu.
Mifukaro ili ndi chine ndipo ndi malo oyambira kuopa chitsiriza cha chitsiriza cha Nyiragongo, komanso kuwononga zikomuza za kudyunsa ziphi mwa ziphi ku Africa.
Usa boda-boda (moto taxi) kuti uli ndikulu m'Goma. Chiphekero chomwe chimathandiza m'malo uno chimatha kukhala ma 500 a Congolese Francs pa ndimbela yakufumbo.
Muli ndi kukwikira kwa kukhala kositezera, "Timbuktu" kwachitika kukhala chizindikiro cha ndalama, ndalama zokhala zafekera.
Naziina, Timbuktu ili chilidwa, koma kuli pa chikhosi chachikulu cha opanga zovisitira, ndipo ili ndi malo owuka.
Muli 1990, ili chikalidwa m'mbenge wa zamabwe zokhala zowononga, chifukwa cha zowononga za m'nyanzi.
Iliyo kuli n'omwe m'abungeni akulu okuli za Henry Louis Gates a PBS special a "Wonders of the African World".
Mifukaso ichi ndi chifukwa choti chimakhala cha kukhala ndi chizindikiro chachikhalidwe cha Akhanasi kupyikiritsa chizindikiro cha Africa kwa mapepala opita m'dziko lonsa.
Kugulu kwa Kruger (KNP) kwaluka kum'gubu wa South Africa ndi kumaphirira m'njira ya Mozambique kukhali m'dongo, Zimbabwe kukhali kukhali, ndipo mugulu wamisala wachisunguko ndi chipiwa cha Crocodile.
Mphuva yomwenga ikukhulupiriza 19,500 km² ndipo ikapulutsidwa m'izoni za nyumba za mtundu 14 osiyanasiyana, zambiri zikubalola ntchito za zamlingaliro osiyanasiyana.
Ili ndi monga chiwonetsetsa chabe cha South Africa ndipo chikukonozwa ngati chinkhwala cha Zivengwe za Chisoswe cha Chachikulu cha Malawi (SANParks).
Muli mbenge ngati monga monga mapepala a South African National Parks, pali ndalama zokwanjira za kuyambitsa ndipo za kuuzumpha pa malo ochengetera.
Ichi chingakhumvana zinkulu kwa munthu kuonse kusankha Wild Card, ichi chikupereka mvekese ku zipeto za mapepala a zamabwe a South Africa kapena mapepala a South African National Parks onse.
Hong Kong Island iliupa chilongwe cha chini cha Hong Kong ndipo ndiyo chikhono chomwe oimbawo ambiri amamwidwa.
Mphula wa mayi a mitungwi omwe amapangira ndalama za Hong Kong amakhulupirika kuti ndi chitsanzo chochokera pa zambonzero zosuka chomwe chimakhala chizimagomezera chifukwa cha madzi a Chinyongwe cha Victoria.

Mphula wa Sundarbans ukukuvulira ifumu ya 3,850 km², ya kuti mapepula a mphesa/nzumbu amagwira mapepula okuyika patsogolo a nkhosi zipitiliza ka chinkhalalo.
Kachi muli muli ku 1966, Sundarbans ili kukhala chibinda cha zamana zamoyo, ndipo kumene kusanka kuti kuli mphwezi 400 a chimbadwe cha Bengal komanso mchengetero wa mapepula 30,000 poyikidwa m'nthawi iyi.
Mapiko amagwirana mwachilichili ku chimbwero cha mapiko okwanjira za mapepala a misoni (ku khaya cha chinyama), koma ambiri, makamaka amene amapanga ku khati, ndi ku Jakar/Bumthang amalowa pakati pa kusaka msanga ndi kusaka msanga.
Chifukwa zikombi zokuthamalira pakati pa zikhumalo zimatha kukhala zinkagwiritsidwa ntchito, ndili chositha kukhala ndi chiti a zikombi zokha mitengo yambiri.
Zimwe zikulu za mapepala zimadwedwa ndi mabuse acomo a Japanese Coaster, omwe ndi odredwa komanso okometsera.
Makhomo a ochuluka amene amaduluka mwachiso ndipo amathandiza kwambiri kulowa mmawa a zikhalidwe zokwanira, monga Paro (Nu 150) ndi Punakha (Nu 200).
Mphu yo Oyapock ya kumagobera ndi mphu ya ma cable-stayed. Ii ikukhulupiriza chinyaruka cha Oyapock likugwiritsa za kumukula mapepala a mapepala a Oiapoque ku Brazil ndi makhosi a Saint-Georges de l'Oyapock ku French Guiana.
Mitengo ichilichilichili ichikulu cha 83 m, ndipo ili 378 m, ndipo ichili mafirigo awiri okhala 3.50 m awiri.
Kukhala m'changu cha chizindikiro cha m'nyumba likuula 15 mita. Kukonzekera kwa kumapanga kwalira mosi mwa August 2011, kusanga anthu m'mpulatsa kunapereka zokwanira m'ndi March 2017.
Mphatso wa chinkhwalitiramo ulikali ukugwira ntchito mchokera ku September 2017, pamene mapepala a zinkhwalitiramo a Brazil amadhwalitsidwa.
Bakwarani anali chikhulu kwambiri among'ono asindika omwe analimira m'Chishiga chichakwera. Anali m'dzimma, alimira pakukhala osiyana ndi kukula kwa miyambo.
Chaco region ili pawoza amaza mitenge ya mabata aza malinga monga Guaycurú ndi Payaguá, omwe anadya ndi kukudikitsa ndi kusunga miyambo ya chiko.

Kukhini ili chikalata chikhalikapo ndipo chiwonelera m'mngani.
Chifukwa chake, kuwerenga chinyorero ichi cha makalumula cha chigwiritsa ntchito, k chitinthu chochitira kuti ufarekezwe kwambiri za machikhalidwe a chigwiritsa ntchito cha Chirisiya ndipo ukombe zifukwa bwino.
Ngasinki, ngati uuli chikalonse cha zamakona, n'otishanyikidwa kusonda chilungano cha Portuguese.
Kweru, anthu opitaza kukonda chikhinyi cha chispania pang'ono amawonera zikwenyeza kuti chisepha cha maputuguese chikukamba bwino, chiyena si chofuna kudyunsa pa chikhinyi chakabwe.
Malu mitandikidwa ku zamankaka m'mbenge m'zanga nthawi zanga zanga m'dzera pa mitandiko ya mmuzimu, kapena monga makhalidwe a kufunika.
Mungenepo wa kuchepetsa chokera m'mphesa minali chisoni chakachulukira chabe, minali nthawi zambiri m'mifukowi kapena m'makona a zikolwa, ndipo minali osavuta kukafika kupweteka zikha zonenekera m'nthawi zatsui.
Zikhalidwe zambiri za zikambere za kufuwa zamagwiritsidwa ntchito kusasa nkhiri zimakhala zinkakhudza mibengo yatsoka m'nthaka osiyanasiyana, ndipo zimakhala zikukulu kwambiri ndipo zimapwirira m'nthawi zolondola za zakudulura.
Kukhala pa chikhuchu cha zinthu zokona za chikhuchu, kumadziwika ngati hanami, kumbali ya zambiri za chienta cha Japanese kupewa chikhulu cha 8.
Mfelowo ilipeza ku China kumene zikhala zikhulupirika m'chizinda chokera ku mfulu.
M'chifumu mwa Japan, zokera zoyambira za kumvetsa mchunga wa mchulpiko zinali zikukonzedwa ndi chikalంతి chokha kwa iye ndi mandima a zamaganu okhawo okhala kumadhira m'ndikong'ano ya kulamulira.
Mizimu iya chiwanga imakhulupira bwino pofuka pa msewu wawo, ngakhale kuti zikuchuluka, ngoma kusayamba kuwon suna zinthu zositali ngakhale "izoyamba" munthu wosuka.

Singapore ndipo muli chikhosi chochokera kwambiri ndipo chifukwa chake chiyenera kusindika, ndipo muli ophatikiza zonse kapena zonse zotengasula kunapita.

Ndimvileza kuti mabusu aiti onapanga amagwira kuHebron koma osayenda ngati kusayerekeza kuKiryat Arba, malo osinga pawo a anthu achisewuti.

Akuwo a kuonse zikambula mbatiti za zokometeka ku msombetsi ndi ku kukotera.
Chifumu cha Chokera ndi chibu cha mapepala achikristu, ndipo chimatchuluka ngati mchithyo wa Yesu Khisite.
Zomwe zambiri za zamphamvu zokhudzana ndi mhenda iyi zakhititsidwa komanso ndi osintha kufingo mamaziko a Khristu ndi osintha kufingo m'dziko lonsolo.
Pamene kukhalapo kulibapa za kukhala zifukwa za chilandwe chogwiritsa ntchito mntsya wa Chivumba kuti wone sunrise.
Ponso pa zamene zikhalili, kusowa zifotokozo za zamene za nfolo za anthu achisristu, koma zithaopa kukhala chitchino cha zamene cha zamene zikhalili cha chisanengalo ndi zokopola.
Zokuti zam'mitengo yachikalonza, mitengo yachikalonza yambili ikunena Chivumbulo cha Chivumbulo pa masiku a chinyolwa, pa zokutse za chinyolwa, ndipo anthu okhudzidwa amawakhala aukamba zokuyeretsedwa pa nkhosi ya mbaso, kuti achiritse chinyerekezo cha chotsechere cha Khristu.
Zikondwe zonse zamadvetera zikaphuka zikabula m'mifukilo zikayuka kapena zikayuka.

Kuchekera pankhulu pa anthu mwa Galapagos, zamunda zambiri zinkayikidwa monga zamunda, zamunda, mafumu, zikole, zikamikanda ndi zikati.

Kutsini ziwine ntchito za zamalawa zili zowenga komanso zokhalira kupwira m'ntchito kumvekera zamalawa.
Zinzumuza zili ndi zida zambiri m'ntchito, ndipo anthu osadga amawadzata ndi mawo awo kapena ma chimpanji awo.
Kukhala ndi chiyembekezo cha ntchito yayang'ana m'nyumba ya ntchito ndi chokamba, chimakhulupiriza za ntchito ya dz$'a gulu ngati chiyembekezo chokometsera ntchito ya monga m'malo mwa kumene mikhalidwe ya ndabu yakhala ikukhudzidwa.
Ofi ndabuwa amene amagwira ntchito amafunika kopa m'nthu oyambitsawo ndikupindika pa zimayambitsa zifukwa zokhala zosonyeza, ndipo amapewa kulinga monga muli m'ndiwo osayidza m'ndiwo ndipo amayamba kudyunsa monga m'ndiwo amamene akukamba.
